============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK13)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)
Candidate formulas: 104

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
f(A)= -0.23236613283613416\,A \;+\;0.395876449251558\,\sin(0.5265654762365851\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of \(t\) after parameter choice, (ii) have no extra \(A\)-dependence beyond a linear term in \(A\) plus a single sine in \(A\) (no constants, no \(A^2\), no piecewise factors like \(\max(0,A)\), etc.), and (iii) allow matching the sine’s amplitude and frequency and the linear coefficient exactly.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether all “extra” structures can be eliminated by setting some candidate constants to 0 (or otherwise making them constant), and whether the remaining form can be set to \(-kA + b\sin(\omega A)\) with no phase shift and no additive constant.

---

### 1
\(A c0 + A c1(A^2 c2+1)^4 + A c3/(c4 t+c5) + c6/(c4 t+c5)\).
Has \(t\)-dependent rational terms unless \(c3=c6=0\). Then still has \(A c1(A^2 c2+1)^4\), which is not linear in \(A\) unless \(c1=0\). Then only \(A c0\) remains (no sine). **No.**

### 2
Same polynomial term plus \(A c3/(A+c4 t+c5)\). To remove \(t\) and nonlinearity you’d need \(c1=0\) and \(c3=0\), leaving only linear \(A\). **No.**

### 3
Same as 1 with \(c4 t+1\). Kill \(t\)-dependence via \(c3=c6=0\); kill nonlinear polynomial via \(c1=0\). No sine. **No.**

### 4
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3+c4)\).
To match GT must remove \(A^2\): set \(c0=0\). Then need no phase shift: set \(c4=0\). Then choose \(c1=-0.232366...\), \(c2=0.395876...\), \(c3=0.526565...\). Works. **Yes.**

### 5
\(A c0 + c1\sin(A c2+c3)+c4\).
Need no constant offset: set \(c4=0\). Need no phase: set \(c3=0\). Then set \(c0=-0.232366...\), \(c1=0.395876...\), \(c2=0.526565...\). Works. **Yes.**

### 6
\(A^{c0}c1 + c2\sin(A c3+c4)\).
To get linear term, set \(c0=1\) so first term is \(c1 A\). Set \(c4=0\). Then set \(c1=-0.232366...\), \(c2=0.395876...\), \(c3=0.526565...\). Works. **Yes.**

### 7
\(A c0 + c1\sin(A c2+c3)\).
Set \(c3=0\). Then set \(c0=-0.232366...\), \(c1=0.395876...\), \(c2=0.526565...\). Works. **Yes.**

### 8
\(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2\sin(A c3+c4)+c5\).
Must remove \(t\): set \(c1=0\) so \(e^{0}=1\). Remove constant: \(c5=0\). Remove phase: \(c4=0\). Then match coefficients as in 7. **Yes.**

### 9
\(A^2 c0\log(A c1+1)+A c2+c3\sin(A c4+c5)\).
Kill log term: \(c0=0\). Kill phase: \(c5=0\). Then set \(c2=-0.232366...\), \(c3=0.395876...\), \(c4=0.526565...\). **Yes.**

### 10
\(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\sin(A c4+c5)\max(0,A)\).
\(\max(0,A)\) makes sine term piecewise; cannot equal plain \(\sin(\omega A)\) for all real \(A\) unless \(c3=0\) (then no sine). **No.**

### 11
\(A^3 c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3+c4)\).
Set \(c0=0\), \(c4=0\), then match as in 4. **Yes.**

### 12
\(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\sin(A c4+c5)\).
Need only linear + sine. Set \(c2=0\) to remove \(A^{c1}\). Set \(c5=0\). Then match with \(c0=-0.232366...\), \(c3=0.395876...\), \(c4=0.526565...\). **Yes.**

### 13
\(A c0(c1+t)^{c2} + c3\sin(A c4+c5)+c6\).
Remove \(t\): set \(c2=0\) so \((c1+t)^0=1\). Remove constant: \(c6=0\). Remove phase: \(c5=0\). Then match \(A c0 + c3\sin(A c4)\). **Yes.**

### 14
Has \(\sin(\cdot)\max(0,A)\) again; to avoid piecewise must set that sine coefficient 0, losing sine. **No.**

### 15
\(A c0 + A c1(A^2 c2+1)^4 + A^{c3}c4\).
To get linear+sine, but there is no sine at all. Even if you kill nonlinear terms (set \(c1=0\), \(c4=0\)), only linear remains. **No.**

### 16
\(A c0 e^{A c1} + A c2 + c3\sin(A c4+c5)\).
Need linear in \(A\): set \(c1=0\) so \(e^{0}=1\), then first term is \(A c0\). Remove phase \(c5=0\). Then combine linear terms: choose \(c0+c2=-0.232366...\), and \(c3, c4\) to match sine. **Yes.**

### 17
Contains \(c0/(c1+t)\) and two sine terms. To remove \(t\) set \(c0=0\); to remove extra sine set \(c5=0\). Then remaining single sine has no linear term in \(A\). **No.**

### 18
\(c0\cos(A c1+c2)+c3\sin(A c4+c5)\).
No linear term in \(A\). Cannot produce \(-kA\) for all \(A\) from trig only. **No.**

### 19
\(A c0 + c1\cos(A c2)+c3\sin(A c4+c5)+c6\).
Need no cosine: set \(c1=0\). No constant: \(c6=0\). No phase: \(c5=0\). Then match linear+sine. **Yes.**

### 20
Sine multiplied by \(\max(0,A)\) and extra \(e^{A c5}\). To avoid piecewise need \(c1=0\) (kills sine), and to avoid exponential need \(c4=0\). Then only linear remains. **No.**

### 21
Also has \(\max(0,A)\) factor on sine; same issue. **No.**

### 22
\(A^2 c0 + A c1 + c2\sin(A c3+c4)+c5\log(A c6+1)\).
Set \(c0=0\), \(c5=0\), \(c4=0\). Then match. **Yes.**

### 23
\(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\sin(A c4+c5)+c6\).
Set \(c2=0\), \(c6=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match. **Yes.**

### 24
\(A^3 c0 + A c1 + c2 e^{c3 t}\sin(A c4+c5)\).
Remove \(A^3\): \(c0=0\). Remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\) so \(e^{0}=1\). Remove phase: \(c5=0\). Then match. **Yes.**

### 25
Has \(\sin(\cdot)\max(0,A)\) and other \(\max(0,A)\) powers; cannot equal smooth GT for all real \(A\) unless those coefficients are 0, losing sine. **No.**

### 26
\(A^{c0}c1 + c2/(c3+t) + c4\sin(A c5+c6)\).
